\doxysubsection{Typedef Documentation}
\Hypertarget{namespace_sentient_a9101e175dfaeb7740209f9a8991083f4}\index{Sentient@{Sentient}!SenContentDeviceID@{SenContentDeviceID}}
\index{SenContentDeviceID@{SenContentDeviceID}!Sentient@{Sentient}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{SenContentDeviceID}{SenContentDeviceID}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespace_sentient_a9101e175dfaeb7740209f9a8991083f4} 
typedef \doxymbox{\hyperlink{_orbis_types_8h_a798af1e30bc65f319c1a246cecf59e39}{DWORD}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespace_sentient_a9101e175dfaeb7740209f9a8991083f4}{Sentient::\+\+Sen\+Content\+Device\+ID}}}



A unique identifier for a device. 

Some routines want to know which device to default to. This ID is a way to specify one. On Xbox, this is equivalent to an \doxylink{extra_x64_8h_a8f15f7b6431e01ac6a3971f0a155df4c}{XCONTENTDEVICEID} and can be obtained in several ways through the XDK. On Windows, this is TBD.

\Hypertarget{namespace_sentient_a38f21c543a8f0c982c9c0ed015dc2308}\index{Sentient@{Sentient}!SenResourceID@{SenResourceID}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{SenResourceID}{SenResourceID}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespace_sentient_a38f21c543a8f0c982c9c0ed015dc2308} 
enum \doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespace_sentient_a38f21c543a8f0c982c9c0ed015dc2308}{Sentient::\+\+Sen\+Resource\+ID}} :\+ INT32}



Resource types/\+categories. 

\doxylink{requirements_The}{The} top 8 bits are always the \doxylink{namespace_sentient_a8caad6615bf878fdc90e749249a657c0}{Sen\+Resource\+Type}. \doxylink{requirements_The}{The} bottom 24 are typically an index into the category. These categories do not overlap, so that we can choose to store different resource types in the same or different tables, depending on what is more useful. Note, though, that you should expect E\+\_\+\+INVALIDARG back if you pass an ID from one category to a call wanting a different category. Some categories\textquotesingle{} IDs will be hardwired/\+assumed, while others will be generated inside of Microsoft (e.\+g. box art). \begin{DoxyEnumFields}[2]{Enumerator}
\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{SenResourceID\_Invalid@{SenResourceID\_Invalid}!Sentient@{Sentient}}

\Hypertarget{namespace_sentient_a6de9084c29c90522df53a7d9f07ffa29}\index{Sentient@{Sentient}!SenSysOfferID@{SenSysOfferID}}
\index{SenSysOfferID@{SenSysOfferID}!Sentient@{Sentient}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{SenSysOfferID}{SenSysOfferID}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespace_sentient_a6de9084c29c90522df53a7d9f07ffa29} 
enum \doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespace_sentient_a6de9084c29c90522df53a7d9f07ffa29}{Sentient::\+\+Sen\+Sys\+Offer\+ID}} :\+ INT64}



A unique identifier for an offer on Xbox/\+\+Windows Live Marketplace. 

This 64-\/bit value may be passed off to system routines that prompt the user to browse/\+buy a product, such as a trial/\+demo or an avatar item. Note that, except for the the special case below, all offer ID values are considered private and should be obtained only through \doxylink{namespace_sentient}{Sentient} APIs and structures. You should never create one manually. \begin{DoxyEnumFields}[2]{Enumerator}

\Hypertarget{namespace_sentient_ac98e2af67a61c3eb8bd46281e1c9d884}\index{Sentient@{Sentient}!SenSysTitleID@{SenSysTitleID}}
\index{SenSysTitleID@{SenSysTitleID}!Sentient@{Sentient}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{SenSysTitleID}{SenSysTitleID}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespace_sentient_ac98e2af67a61c3eb8bd46281e1c9d884} 
enum \doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespace_sentient_ac98e2af67a61c3eb8bd46281e1c9d884}{Sentient::\+\+Sen\+Sys\+Title\+ID}} :\+ INT32}



A unique identifier per title. 

Each title on Xbox Live is given a 32-\/bit title ID. We use these to help identify title-\/specific resourced, UGC, etc. Note that, except for the two special cases below, all title ID values are considered private and should be obtained only through \doxylink{namespace_sentient}{Sentient} APIs and structures. You should never create one manually. \begin{DoxyEnumFields}[2]{Enumerator}
\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{SenSysTitleID\_This@{SenSysTitleID\_This}!Sentient@{Sentient}}

\Hypertarget{namespace_sentient_a1bf2f31f8ec0908ebb4c0d2a4860278a}\index{Sentient@{Sentient}!SenAcknowledgeVIPLevelChange@{SenAcknowledgeVIPLevelChange}}
\index{SenAcknowledgeVIPLevelChange@{SenAcknowledgeVIPLevelChange}!Sentient@{Sentient}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{SenAcknowledgeVIPLevelChange()}{SenAcknowledgeVIPLevelChange()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespace_sentient_a1bf2f31f8ec0908ebb4c0d2a4860278a} 
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{_orbis_types_8h_a3cc49f3164c43289d0bcb2abafc399bc}{HRESULT}} Sentient::\+\+Sen\+Acknowledge\+VIPLevel\+Change (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{user\+Index}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Acknowledge a change in user VIP level reported by the server. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\doxymbox{\texttt{in}}  & {\em user\+Index} & \doxylink{requirements_The}{The} index of the initiating user on the console. Note:\+ This is NOT a XUID.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Check \doxylink{_orbis_2_orbis_extras_2winerror_8h_a1eff4fb052d6e497649f6a06b4ac222a}{SUCCEEDED( hresult )} or \doxylink{_orbis_stubs_8h_aca3919e6cf22894d07999a67e24bfded}{FAILED( hresult )} to determine success. Specific values include:\+ SENTIENT\+\_\+\+E\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED:\+ You did not call \doxylink{namespace_sentient_a3d8681ebb382655d1e8946b73fd89124}{Sentient\+Initialize()} first. SENTIENT\+\_\+\+E\+\_\+\+GUEST\+\_\+\+ACCESS\+\_\+\+VIOLATION:\+ A guest may not spawn this call. E\+\_\+\+FAIL:\+ Failed to spawn server call. S\+\_\+\+OK:\+ Server call spawned successfully.
\end{DoxyReturn}
When retrieving user VIP status, the server will include the user\textquotesingle{}s last VIP level for which it has not received an acknowledgement message. Titles can use this information to highlight changes in VIP level. Once a change has been messaged titles should call this API to clear the server state. \Hypertarget{namespace_sentient_a4b21d8f88c1db839f46ecd4c54f29792}\index{Sentient@{Sentient}!SenAvatarDownloadXML@{SenAvatarDownloadXML}}
\index{SenAvatarDownloadXML@{SenAvatarDownloadXML}!Sentient@{Sentient}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{SenFlushFameProgress()}{SenFlushFameProgress()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespace_sentient_acf58d31e7e621d69ca8bc340dbd9a81a} 
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{_orbis_types_8h_a3cc49f3164c43289d0bcb2abafc399bc}{HRESULT}} Sentient::\+\+Sen\+Flush\+Fame\+Progress (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{user\+Index}{, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespace_sentient_ae7d4d8ba3de5536257cd02af2fca4f4c}{Sen\+Sys\+Completed\+Callback}}}]{user\+Callback}{, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{_durango_2_miles_2include_2mss_8h_afed5b2f9cfdce0d76b8a9e307d336b91}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{user\+Callback\+Data}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Ensure that all progress writes are committed to the \doxylink{namespace_sentient}{Sentient} server. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\doxymbox{\texttt{in}}  & {\em user\+Index} & \doxylink{requirements_The}{The} index of the initiating user on the console. Note:\+ This is NOT a XUID.\\
\hline
\doxymbox{\texttt{in}}  & {\em \doxylink{namespace_sentient_a8aea1736144789afc1c3aa7a67773db2}{user\+Callback}} & If this call returns a success code, the user\+Callback will be called at the end of the asynchronous process.\\
\hline
\doxymbox{\texttt{in}}  & {\em \doxylink{namespace_sentient_a43bb9b3e6a790f24ebedbc4c70cba012}{user\+Callback\+Data}} & Data to be passed to the {\itshape user\+Callback} on completion.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Check \doxylink{_orbis_2_orbis_extras_2winerror_8h_a1eff4fb052d6e497649f6a06b4ac222a}{SUCCEEDED( hresult )} or \doxylink{_orbis_stubs_8h_aca3919e6cf22894d07999a67e24bfded}{FAILED( hresult )} to determine success. Specific values include:\+ SENTIENT\+\_\+\+E\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED:\+ You did not call \doxylink{namespace_sentient_a3d8681ebb382655d1e8946b73fd89124}{Sentient\+Initialize()} first. SENTIENT\+\_\+\+E\+\_\+\+GUEST\+\_\+\+ACCESS\+\_\+\+VIOLATION:\+ A guest may not spawn this call. SENTIENT\+\_\+\+E\+\_\+\+TOO\+\_\+\+MANY\+\_\+\+CALLS:\+ This call has been rejected to avoid excessive server load. Try again later. E\+\_\+\+FAIL:\+ Failed to spawn server call. This may be because there is already a flush scheduled. S\+\_\+\+OK:\+ \doxylink{requirements_The}{The} operation completed successfully.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Long-\/term storage for progress exists on the \doxylink{namespace_sentient}{Sentient} server, but it may be buffered on the client to prevent excessive server load. Titles should call this API as appropriate (e.\+g. on game save) to ensure that all progress writes are committed to the server. \doxylink{requirements_The}{The} callback parameters provide a mechanism for detecting when the server call has completed and updating user interface appropriately. When there is no local data that needs flushing, the supplied callback will be invoked before execution returns from this function, and the return code will be S\+\_\+\+OK. \Hypertarget{namespace_sentient_af3f66c0fe3acc81d55967b8cc2ac9b89}\index{Sentient@{Sentient}!SenGetAwardMessage@{SenGetAwardMessage}}
\index{SenGetAwardMessage@{SenGetAwardMessage}!Sentient@{Sentient}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{SenGetAwardMessage()}{SenGetAwardMessage()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespace_sentient_af3f66c0fe3acc81d55967b8cc2ac9b89} 
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{_orbis_types_8h_a3cc49f3164c43289d0bcb2abafc399bc}{HRESULT}} Sentient::\+\+Sen\+Get\+Award\+Message (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{user\+Index}{, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{struct_sentient_1_1_sen_award_message_data}{Sen\+Award\+Message\+Data}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{out\+\_\+award\+Data}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Poll for notifications of when a user passes a Fame milestone. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\doxymbox{\texttt{in}}  & {\em user\+Index} & \doxylink{requirements_The}{The} index of the initiating user on the console. Note:\+ This is NOT a XUID.\\
\hline
\doxymbox{\texttt{out}}  & {\em \doxylink{namespace_sentient_afe65beb1f43a02c706ffcd1b59de9936}{out\+\_\+award\+Data}} & Structure to fill in with information about any new award.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
SENTIENT\+\_\+\+E\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED:\+ You did not call \doxylink{namespace_sentient_a3d8681ebb382655d1e8946b73fd89124}{Sentient\+Initialize()} first. SENTIENT\+\_\+\+E\+\_\+\+GUEST\+\_\+\+ACCESS\+\_\+\+VIOLATION:\+ A guest may not spawn this call. E\+\_\+\+POINTER:\+ out\+\_\+award\+Data is nullptr. SENTIENT\+\_\+\+S\+\_\+\+OPERATION\+\_\+\+IN\+\_\+\+PROGRESS:\+ \doxylink{requirements_The}{The} call could not be completed immediately and out\+\_\+award\+Data has not been filled in. S\+\_\+\+FALSE:\+ \doxylink{requirements_The}{The} operation completed successfully but there were no awards to report. out\+\_\+award\+Data has not been filled in. S\+\_\+\+OK:\+ \doxylink{requirements_The}{The} operation completed successfully and there was a valid award to report. out\+\_\+award\+Data contains information about the award.
\end{DoxyReturn}
There are no restrictions on how frequently this API may be called, and it returnes immediately, so titles should poll in all states where they can display award messages. When a message is returned it is popped from an internal queue and will not be returned again by further calls. \Hypertarget{namespace_sentient_aba0c380ff623336b79482d5f64b5f58d}\index{Sentient@{Sentient}!SenGetFameDisplayData@{SenGetFameDisplayData}}
\index{SenGetFameDisplayData@{SenGetFameDisplayData}!Sentient@{Sentient}}

Retrieve a summary of a user\textquotesingle{}s progress against Fame Challenges. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\doxymbox{\texttt{in}}  & {\em user\+Index} & \doxylink{requirements_The}{The} index of the initiating user on the console. Note:\+ This is NOT a XUID.\\

 This parameter can be used to support results paging.\\

It is assumed that this is preallocated to at least {\itshape max\+Display\+Data\+Count} entries.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Check \doxylink{_orbis_2_orbis_extras_2winerror_8h_a1eff4fb052d6e497649f6a06b4ac222a}{SUCCEEDED( hresult )} or \doxylink{_orbis_stubs_8h_aca3919e6cf22894d07999a67e24bfded}{FAILED( hresult )} to determine success. Specific values include:\+ SENTIENT\+\_\+\+E\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED:\+ You did not call \doxylink{namespace_sentient_a3d8681ebb382655d1e8946b73fd89124}{Sentient\+Initialize()} first. SENTIENT\+\_\+\+E\+\_\+\+GUEST\+\_\+\+ACCESS\+\_\+\+VIOLATION:\+ A guest may not spawn this call. E\+\_\+\+POINTER:\+ out\+\_\+data\+Count or out\+\_\+display\+Data is nullptr. E\+\_\+\+INVALIDARG:\+ start\+Index is greater than the total number of items available. SENTIENT\+\_\+\+S\+\_\+\+OPERATION\+\_\+\+IN\+\_\+\+PROGRESS:\+ \doxylink{requirements_The}{The} call could not be completed immediately and output parameters have not been filled in. E\+\_\+\+FAIL:\+ \doxylink{namespace_internal}{Internal} failure. Check log for output. S\+\_\+\+OK:\+ \doxylink{requirements_The}{The} operation completed successfully.
\end{DoxyReturn}
For titles with weekly Challenge rotations, only Challenges active for the current week are reported. Use \doxylink{namespace_sentient_a01647e6206582b68557692d7c20b99f6}{Sen\+Get\+Fame\+Display\+Data\+Count()} to dynamically size a buffer large enough to obtain all the display data entries in a single call, or use the start\+Index parameter for paging. \Hypertarget{namespace_sentient_a01647e6206582b68557692d7c20b99f6}\index{Sentient@{Sentient}!SenGetFameDisplayDataCount@{SenGetFameDisplayDataCount}}
\index{SenGetFameDisplayDataCount@{SenGetFameDisplayDataCount}!Sentient@{Sentient}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{SenGetFameDisplayDataCount()}{SenGetFameDisplayDataCount()}}

Titles can use this API to ensure that they allocate a buffer of appropriate size before making a call to Sen\+Get\+Fame\+Display\+Data. \Hypertarget{namespace_sentient_a4f691cd8c8c2dccaedc26ac0cdbafe94}\index{Sentient@{Sentient}!SenGetFameLeaderboard@{SenGetFameLeaderboard}}

Query a Fame leaderboard. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}

\doxymbox{\texttt{in}}  & {\em entry\+Count\+Max} & \doxylink{requirements_The}{The} maximum number of leaderboard rows to return.\\
\hline
\doxymbox{\texttt{out}}  & {\em out\+\_\+entry\+Array} & \doxylink{requirements_The}{The} structures to fill in with the rows returned from the leaderboard query. It is assumed that this is preallocated to hold at least entry\+Count\+Max entries.\\
\hline
\doxymbox{\texttt{out}}  & {\em out\+\_\+leaderboard\+Results} & Summary information about the results of the leaderboard query.\\
\hline
\doxymbox{\texttt{out}}  & {\em \doxylink{namespace_sentient_a1a75541e5f3b88946839e3018f3350a3}{out\+\_\+sen\+Handle}} & Provides a handle to the async task, which will allow for calling Sentient\+Cancel\\
\hline
\doxymbox{\texttt{in}}  & {\em \doxylink{namespace_sentient_a8aea1736144789afc1c3aa7a67773db2}{user\+Callback}} & If this call returns a success code, the user\+Callback will be called at the end of the asynchronous process.\\
\hline
\doxymbox{\texttt{in}}  & {\em \doxylink{namespace_sentient_a43bb9b3e6a790f24ebedbc4c70cba012}{user\+Callback\+Data}} & Data to be passed to the {\itshape user\+Callback} on completion.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

Specific values include:\+ SENTIENT\+\_\+\+E\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED:\+ You did not call \doxylink{namespace_sentient_a3d8681ebb382655d1e8946b73fd89124}{Sentient\+Initialize()} first. SENTIENT\+\_\+\+E\+\_\+\+GUEST\+\_\+\+ACCESS\+\_\+\+VIOLATION:\+ A guest may not spawn this call. E\+\_\+\+POINTER:\+ out\+\_\+entry\+Array or out\+\_\+leaderboard\+Results is nullptr. E\+\_\+\+INVALIDARG:\+ user\+Callback is nullptr and out\+\_\+sen\+Handle is non-\/nullptr. Task handles are not supported for synchronous requests. SENTIENT\+\_\+\+E\+\_\+\+TOO\+\_\+\+MANY\+\_\+\+CALLS:\+ This call has been rejected to avoid excessive server load. Try again later. E\+\_\+\+FAIL:\+ Failed to spawn server call. S\+\_\+\+OK:\+ Server call spawned successfully. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

This overload is preferred when retrieving information about local users. There are no restrictions on the call frequency and it will typically return immediately. In rare cases where SENTIENT\+\_\+\+S\+\_\+\+OPERATION\+\_\+\+IN\+\_\+\+PROGRESS is returned the title should call again on the next scheduled iteration of their \doxylink{namespace_sentient}{Sentient} update loop. \Hypertarget{namespace_sentient_a3c4c6691f92398612bafb941f196993f}\index{Sentient@{Sentient}!SenGetFameVIPLevel@{SenGetFameVIPLevel}}

\doxymbox{\texttt{out}}  & {\em \doxylink{namespace_sentient_a3d48457e6f460b66e615ca7e5f78d61b}{out\+\_\+name}} & \doxylink{requirements_The}{The} string to fill in with the VIP level name. It is assumed that this is preallocated to fit at least {\itshape max\+Name\+Length} characters.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Check \doxylink{_orbis_2_orbis_extras_2winerror_8h_a1eff4fb052d6e497649f6a06b4ac222a}{SUCCEEDED( hresult )} or \doxylink{_orbis_stubs_8h_aca3919e6cf22894d07999a67e24bfded}{FAILED( hresult )} to determine success. Specific values include:\+ SENTIENT\+\_\+\+E\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED:\+ You did not call \doxylink{namespace_sentient_a3d8681ebb382655d1e8946b73fd89124}{Sentient\+Initialize()} first. E\+\_\+\+POINTER:\+ out\+\_\+name is nullptr. E\+\_\+\+INVALIDARG:\+ vip\+Level is outside the range of known VIP levels. SENTIENT\+\_\+\+S\+\_\+\+OPERATION\+\_\+\+IN\+\_\+\+PROGRESS:\+ \doxylink{requirements_The}{The} call could not be completed immediately and out\+\_\+name has not been filled in. S\+\_\+\+OK:\+ \doxylink{requirements_The}{The} operation completed successfully.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Titles can use this API to get the server-\/defined name for a VIP level for additional flexibility post-\/release. In rare cases where SENTIENT\+\_\+\+S\+\_\+\+OPERATION\+\_\+\+IN\+\_\+\+PROGRESS is returned the title should call again on the next scheduled iteration of their \doxylink{namespace_sentient}{Sentient} update loop. \Hypertarget{namespace_sentient_a704f9b88210a395b23386b8dcef52266}\index{Sentient@{Sentient}!SenMarkerAdd@{SenMarkerAdd}}

Inform the \doxylink{namespace_sentient}{Sentient} server about the results of a multiplayer game. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\doxymbox{\texttt{in}}  & {\em user\+Index} & \doxylink{requirements_The}{The} index of the initiating user on the console. Note:\+ This is NOT a XUID.\\
\hline
\doxymbox{\texttt{in}}  & {\em participant\+Count} & \doxylink{requirements_The}{The} number of valid items in {\itshape participants}.\\
\hline
\doxymbox{\texttt{in}}  & {\em participants} & Structures describing the users who participated in this multiplayer game.\\
\hline
\doxymbox{\texttt{out}}  & {\em \doxylink{namespace_sentient_a1a75541e5f3b88946839e3018f3350a3}{out\+\_\+sen\+Handle}} & Provides a handle to the async task, which will allow for calling Sentient\+Cancel\\
\hline
\doxymbox{\texttt{in}}  & {\em \doxylink{namespace_sentient_a8aea1736144789afc1c3aa7a67773db2}{user\+Callback}} & If this call returns a success code, the user\+Callback will be called at the end of the asynchronous process.\\
\hline
\doxymbox{\texttt{in}}  & {\em \doxylink{namespace_sentient_a43bb9b3e6a790f24ebedbc4c70cba012}{user\+Callback\+Data}} & Data to be passed to the {\itshape user\+Callback} on completion. ~\newline
\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Check \doxylink{_orbis_2_orbis_extras_2winerror_8h_a1eff4fb052d6e497649f6a06b4ac222a}{SUCCEEDED( hresult )} or \doxylink{_orbis_stubs_8h_aca3919e6cf22894d07999a67e24bfded}{FAILED( hresult )} to determine success. Specific values include:\+ SENTIENT\+\_\+\+E\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED:\+ You did not call \doxylink{namespace_sentient_a3d8681ebb382655d1e8946b73fd89124}{Sentient\+Initialize()} first. SENTIENT\+\_\+\+E\+\_\+\+GUEST\+\_\+\+ACCESS\+\_\+\+VIOLATION:\+ A guest may not spawn this call. E\+\_\+\+INVALIDARG:\+ Either user\+Callback is nullptr and out\+\_\+sen\+Handle is non-\/nullptr, or participant\+Count is less than 2. E\+\_\+\+POINTER:\+ participants is nullptr. E\+\_\+\+FAIL:\+ Failed to spawn server call. S\+\_\+\+OK:\+ Server call spawned successfully.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Titles should report multiplayer sessions to the \doxylink{namespace_sentient}{Sentient} server via this API in order to support tracking of progress against certain Fame Challenges. For proper tracking each user in the multiplayer session should independently call this function on completion of a game. \Hypertarget{namespace_sentient_a01424383545b1809420e786bb52737b5}\index{Sentient@{Sentient}!SenSetUserLeaderboardValue@{SenSetUserLeaderboardValue}}

Requests that \doxylink{namespace_sentient}{Sentient} immediately send any stats being buffered. 

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

SENTIENT\+\_\+\+E\+\_\+\+TOO\+\_\+\+MANY\+\_\+\+CALLS:\+ You tried to flush too quickly after a previous flush. S\+\_\+\+OK:\+ Buffered stats will be flushed to the server on the next Sentient::\+\+Update() call
\end{DoxyReturn}
This API can only be called once every minute. Any attempts to call the API more frequently will result in the call being throttled, and the API returning SENTIENT\+\_\+\+E\+\_\+\+TOO\+\_\+\+MANY\+\_\+\+CALLS Data is not actually sent until the next Sentient::\+\+Update() call \Hypertarget{namespace_sentient_ac1db3c43389abcd6d4d9b8f88f6f5b5c}\index{Sentient@{Sentient}!SentientFlushStatsOnExit@{SentientFlushStatsOnExit}}

Tells \doxylink{namespace_sentient}{Sentient} that an important point in the game was hit and that events should be sent as soon as possible. 

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Check \doxylink{_orbis_2_orbis_extras_2winerror_8h_a1eff4fb052d6e497649f6a06b4ac222a}{SUCCEEDED( hresult )} or \doxylink{_orbis_stubs_8h_aca3919e6cf22894d07999a67e24bfded}{FAILED( hresult )} to determine success. S\+\_\+\+OK:\+ Buffered stats will be flushed to the server within the next minute
\end{DoxyReturn}
This API should be caleld when the game hits an important event or point. \doxylink{namespace_sentient}{Sentient} Will send the event data to the server within the next minute, calling this method frequently will not cause any additional sends \Hypertarget{namespace_sentient_a7a1630f719622544f8f14c7755e69444}\index{Sentient@{Sentient}!SentientFlushStatsOnMarketPlace@{SentientFlushStatsOnMarketPlace}}

Check \doxylink{_orbis_2_orbis_extras_2winerror_8h_a1eff4fb052d6e497649f6a06b4ac222a}{SUCCEEDED( hresult )} or \doxylink{_orbis_stubs_8h_aca3919e6cf22894d07999a67e24bfded}{FAILED( hresult )} to determine success. Specific values include:\+ SENTIENT\+\_\+\+E\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED:\+ You did not call \doxylink{namespace_sentient_a3d8681ebb382655d1e8946b73fd89124}{Sentient\+Initialize()} first. SENTIENT\+\_\+\+E\+\_\+\+TOO\+\_\+\+MANY\+\_\+\+CALLS:\+ You tried to flush on Market\+Place too many times S\+\_\+\+OK:\+ Buffered stats will be flushed to the server on the next Sentient::\+\+Update() call
\end{DoxyReturn}
Any attempts to call the API too frequently will result in the call being throttled, and the API returning SENTIENT\+\_\+\+E\+\_\+\+TOO\+\_\+\+MANY\+\_\+\+CALLS Data is not actually sent until the next Sentient::\+\+Update() call \Hypertarget{namespace_sentient_a3d8681ebb382655d1e8946b73fd89124}\index{Sentient@{Sentient}!SentientInitialize@{SentientInitialize}}
\index{SentientInitialize@{SentientInitialize}!Sentient@{Sentient}}

Specific values include:\+ E\+\_\+\+FAIL (and other E\+\_\+\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} codes):\+ Failed to initialize. S\+\_\+\+OK:\+ Initialized successfully.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\doxymbox{\texttt{in}}  & {\em p\+Stat} & \doxylink{requirements_The}{The} pointer to \doxylink{struct_sentient_1_1_sen_stat}{Sen\+Stat} structure. \doxylink{requirements_The}{The} Sentient\+Stats\+Send function is usually called from the autogenerated fuctions which use as \+[in]\+ parameters the user\+Index(0 through 3) and the set of the stat properties/\+values. \doxylink{requirements_The}{The} rest of the \doxylink{struct_sentient_1_1_sen_stat}{Sen\+Stat} structure memebers are created automatically from the stat xml file generated code. ~\newline

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespace_sentient_a79c531dd5991027ca6c715dbdf3141eb} 
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{_orbis_types_8h_a3cc49f3164c43289d0bcb2abafc399bc}{HRESULT}} Sentient::\+\+Sentient\+Update (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Update \doxylink{namespace_sentient}{Sentient}\textquotesingle{}s internal state. 

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Check \doxylink{_orbis_2_orbis_extras_2winerror_8h_a1eff4fb052d6e497649f6a06b4ac222a}{SUCCEEDED( hresult )} or \doxylink{_orbis_stubs_8h_aca3919e6cf22894d07999a67e24bfded}{FAILED( hresult )} to determine overall success. \doxylink{requirements_The}{The} return code contains information about the status of the connection to sentient, including:\+ S\+\_\+\+OK:\+ we have a working connection to the \doxylink{namespace_sentient}{Sentient} server. SENTIENT\+\_\+\+S\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+SIGNED\+\_\+\+IN\+\_\+\+TO\+\_\+\+LIVE:\+ no live enabled user user is currently signed in to live. SENTIENT\+\_\+\+S\+\_\+\+INITIALIZING\+\_\+\+CONNECTION:\+ a user has signed in, and we have started first connection attempt, but we have neither succeeded nor failed yet. SENTIENT\+\_\+\+S\+\_\+\+SERVER\+\_\+\+CONNECTION\+\_\+\+FAILED:\+ a connection attempt has failed, or that an existing connection was lost.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Call this every frame to handle network message pumping and to trigger asynchronous callbacks on completed ( or failed ) tasks. \Hypertarget{namespace_sentient_ab99d584f97c03378221717f3419b84b9}\index{Sentient@{Sentient}!SenUGCAddToCustomCounters@{SenUGCAddToCustomCounters}}

\Hypertarget{namespace_sentient_a7a44f50368406a06c8f3384dd6d2f2ac}\index{Sentient@{Sentient}!SenUpdateFameProgress@{SenUpdateFameProgress}}
\index{SenUpdateFameProgress@{SenUpdateFameProgress}!Sentient@{Sentient}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{SenUpdateFameProgress()}{SenUpdateFameProgress()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespace_sentient_a7a44f50368406a06c8f3384dd6d2f2ac} 
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{_orbis_types_8h_a3cc49f3164c43289d0bcb2abafc399bc}{HRESULT}} Sentient::\+\+Sen\+Update\+Fame\+Progress (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{user\+Index}{, }\item[{unsigned int}]{milestone\+Type\+ID}{, }\item[{unsigned int}]{xp\+Gained}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Notify \doxylink{namespace_sentient}{Sentient} about user progress against a Fame Challenge. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\doxymbox{\texttt{in}}  & {\em user\+Index} & \doxylink{requirements_The}{The} index of the initiating user on the console. Note:\+ This is NOT a XUID.\\
\hline
\doxymbox{\texttt{in}}  & {\em milestone\+Type\+ID} & \doxylink{requirements_The}{The} id of the Challenge for which progress has been achieved.\\
\hline
\doxymbox{\texttt{in}}  & {\em xp\+Gained} & Incremental progress. For binary milestones this can be safely set to 1 each time the awarding event takes place.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Check \doxylink{_orbis_2_orbis_extras_2winerror_8h_a1eff4fb052d6e497649f6a06b4ac222a}{SUCCEEDED( hresult )} or \doxylink{_orbis_stubs_8h_aca3919e6cf22894d07999a67e24bfded}{FAILED( hresult )} to determine success. Specific values include:\+ SENTIENT\+\_\+\+E\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED:\+ You did not call \doxylink{namespace_sentient_a3d8681ebb382655d1e8946b73fd89124}{Sentient\+Initialize()} first. SENTIENT\+\_\+\+E\+\_\+\+GUEST\+\_\+\+ACCESS\+\_\+\+VIOLATION:\+ A guest may not spawn this call. SENTIENT\+\_\+\+E\+\_\+\+BUFFER\+\_\+\+EXHAUSTED:\+ \doxylink{requirements_The}{The} progress update failed because \doxylink{namespace_sentient}{Sentient}\textquotesingle{}s internal buffer is full. E\+\_\+\+FAIL:\+ \doxylink{namespace_internal}{Internal} failure. Check log for output. S\+\_\+\+OK:\+ \doxylink{requirements_The}{The} operation completed successfully.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Titles should call this API whenever a user makes progress against a Fame Challenge. Long-\/term storage for progress exists on the \doxylink{namespace_sentient}{Sentient} server, but it may be buffered on the client to prevent excessive server load. Titles should call Sen\+Flush\+Fame\+Progress as appropriate (e.\+g. on game save) to ensure that all progress writes are committed to the server. Titles should not submit updates against Fame Challenges whose progress is determined by the server(e.\+g. First Play) \Hypertarget{namespace_sentient_a86c6370e379b41bb5a745d82d0604643}\index{Sentient@{Sentient}!SenUserIsInRole@{SenUserIsInRole}}

\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxymbox{\hyperlink{_orbis_types_8h_a3cc49f3164c43289d0bcb2abafc399bc}{HRESULT}} Sentient::\+\+Set\+Current\+Culture (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{sal_8h_a3f6b8655e1aa9dfc15a9029f0343009e}{\+\_\+\+\_\+in}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{_orbis_types_8h_a798af1e30bc65f319c1a246cecf59e39}{DWORD}}}]{dw\+Language}{, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{sal_8h_a3f6b8655e1aa9dfc15a9029f0343009e}{\+\_\+\+\_\+in}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{_orbis_types_8h_a798af1e30bc65f319c1a246cecf59e39}{DWORD}}}]{dw\+Locale}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Set the current culture to the one specified, if possible. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\doxymbox{\texttt{in}}  & {\em dw\+Language} & the \doxylink{_orbis_types_8h_a798af1e30bc65f319c1a246cecf59e39}{DWORD} id as defined in xconfig.\+h (e.\+g. XC\+\_\+\+LANGUAGE\+\_\+\+ENGLISH) for the language to use \\
\hline
\doxymbox{\texttt{in}}  & {\em dw\+Locale} & the \doxylink{_orbis_types_8h_a798af1e30bc65f319c1a246cecf59e39}{DWORD} id as defined in xconfig.\+h (e.\+g. XC\+\_\+\+LOCALE\+\_\+\+GREAT\+\_\+\+BRITAIN) for the region to use\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Check \doxylink{_orbis_2_orbis_extras_2winerror_8h_a1eff4fb052d6e497649f6a06b4ac222a}{SUCCEEDED( hresult )} or \doxylink{_orbis_stubs_8h_aca3919e6cf22894d07999a67e24bfded}{FAILED( hresult )} to determine success. Specific values include:\+ SENTIENT\+\_\+\+E\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED:\+ You did not call \doxylink{namespace_sentient_a3d8681ebb382655d1e8946b73fd89124}{Sentient\+Initialize()} first. E\+\_\+\+FAIL:\+ Failed to find the given culture. S\+\_\+\+OK:\+ Current culture set successfully.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Set the current culture to the one specified, if possible (if not english will be used). This should only be called during title launch if it is determined that the console is set to a lanuage unsupported by the title. This method should only be called once, right after calling \doxylink{namespace_sentient_a3d8681ebb382655d1e8946b73fd89124}{Sentient\+Initialize()} This is the culture that will be used when any string routine is called. By default, this is set to the system culture \& region. \Hypertarget{namespace_sentient_a04621463f28107c8d124288c265fd6a2}\index{Sentient@{Sentient}!SetCurrentCultureEnglish@{SetCurrentCultureEnglish}}
\index{SetCurrentCultureEnglish@{SetCurrentCultureEnglish}!Sentient@{Sentient}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{SetCurrentCultureEnglish()}{SetCurrentCultureEnglish()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespace_sentient_a04621463f28107c8d124288c265fd6a2} 
\+\_\+\+\_\+inline \doxymbox{\hyperlink{_orbis_types_8h_a3cc49f3164c43289d0bcb2abafc399bc}{HRESULT}} Sentient::\+\+Set\+Current\+Culture\+English (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Set the current culture to English (no region). 

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Check \doxylink{_orbis_2_orbis_extras_2winerror_8h_a1eff4fb052d6e497649f6a06b4ac222a}{SUCCEEDED( hresult )} or \doxylink{_orbis_stubs_8h_aca3919e6cf22894d07999a67e24bfded}{FAILED( hresult )} to determine success. Specific values include:\+ SENTIENT\+\_\+\+E\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED:\+ You did not call \doxylink{namespace_sentient_a3d8681ebb382655d1e8946b73fd89124}{Sentient\+Initialize()} first. E\+\_\+\+FAIL:\+ Failed to find the given culture. S\+\_\+\+OK:\+ Current culture set successfully.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Set the current culture English. This should only be called during title launch if it is determined that the console is set to a lanuage unsupported by the title. This method should only be called once, right after calling \doxylink{namespace_sentient_a3d8681ebb382655d1e8946b73fd89124}{Sentient\+Initialize()} This is the culture that will be used when any string routine is called. By default, \doxylink{namespace_sentient}{Sentient} uses the console\textquotesingle{}s culture \& region.
